'bras zhugs lhag ma gnyis kyi mngon rtogs nyan thos kyi sa zhes gcig tu byas pa rang rgyal gyi rtogs pa rnams /
rang rgyal gyi sa /
byang sems kyi sa dgu pa man chad byang sems kyi sar byas nas 'da' bya sa dgur 'dren pa'i phyir /
'dren tshul de ltar byas na 'da' bya sa dgu la nyan thos kyi sa dang /
rang rgyal gyi sa byang chub sems dpa'i sa gsum 'dren pa'i rgyu mtshan yod de /
sa bcu par theg pa gsum gyi rtogs rigs yar ldan gyi tshul gyi rdzogs par shes pa'i phyir du yin pa'i phyir /
sa bcu pa'i ye shes la sangs rgyas kyi sa zhes 'chad pa'i rgyu mtshan yod de /
rjes thob kyi skabs su gzhan don byed pa'i sgo nas sangs rgyas dang mnyam pa thob pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis de ltar bshad pa'i phyir /
!mthong dang sgom pa'i lam dag la / /
zhes sogs kyi skabs su /
rang gi ngos skal gyi sgrib gnyis kyi sa bon dngos su 'joms byed kyi sems dpa'i ye shes /
'dir dngos bstan gyi gnyen po'i tshogs sgrub kyi mtshan nyid /
de la dbye na /
mthong spangs gnyen po'i tshogs sgrub dang /
sgom spangs gnyen po'i tshogs sgrub gnyis /
rang gi ngos skal gyi sgrib gnyis mthong spangs dngos su 'joms byed kyi theg chen gyi bar chad med lam /
dngos @# / /
bstan gyi mthong spangs gnyen po'i tshogs sgrub kyi mtshan nyid /
de la spang bya'i gtso bo shes sgrib gzung 'dzin gyi rnam par rtog pa bzhi'i sgo nas dbye ba rnam pa bzhi yang /
rang gi ngos skal gyi sgrib pa lhan skyes dngos su 'joms byed kyi theg chen gyi bar chad med mal 'dir dngos bstan gyi sgom spangs gnyen po'i tshogs sgrub kyi mtshan nyid /
de la yang sgom spangs gzung 'dzin gyi rnam rtag bzhi'i sgo nas rnam pa bzhi yod /
dngos bstan la de ltar yin gyi /
spyir theg chen gyi mthong lam la mthong spangs gnyen po'i tshogs sgrub kyis khyab cing /
sgom lam la yang sgom spangs gnyen po'i tshogs sgrub yin pas khyab bo / /
!ched du bya dang mnyam nyid dang / /
zhes sogs kyi skabs su /
rang 'bras rnam khyen gdon mi za bar nges par 'byin par byed pa'i dag sa'i ye shes /
des 'byung sgrub pa'i mtshan nyid /
de la dbye na /
nges par 'byung ba brgyad kyi sgo nas brgyad yod /
nges par 'byung ba brgyad yod de /
chen pa gsum gcig tu byas pa dang /
sems chen po'i khyad par gsum /
spong ba chen po'i khyad par gnyis /
rtogs pa chen po'i khyad par gnyis dang bcas pa'i brgyad yod pa'i phyir /
nges par 'byung ba brgyad du nges pa yin te /
brgyad po de las khyad par du 'phags pa'i nges par 'byung ba med pa'i phyir /
rab 'byams zhing gi rgyal dang de sras kyis / /
legs par bsngags pa'i rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi / /
sbas don mngon rtogs rim pa lung rigs kyis / /
rdzogs par 'grel ba rje btsun gzhung lugs mchog /
tshul bzhin 'grel mdzad 'phags seng rnam gnyis kyis / /
'grel mdzad gzhan dang thun mong ma yin pa / /
blo bzang grags pa'i lugs bzang rmad du byung / /
de phyir mgon de'i bka' drin bsam mi khyab / /
de bsab phyir du don gnyer 'ga' zhig la / /
phan par srid snyam spyi don 'di byas so / /
de phyir gzur gnas blo gros ldan rnams kyis / /
rnyed bkur don gnyer dri mas ma gos par / /
rang gzhan don gnyes bsgrub par bya ba'i phyir / /
'jug dgos 'di la thos bsam sgom gsum gyis / /
'jug par rigs so brtson pas stobs bskyed cig /
'on kyang bdag ni blo dman brtson pa chung / /
zab mo'i lam 'di rtags par shin tu dka' / /
de'i phyir bdag blo ku sha'i rtse mo yis / /
gzhal nus min yang cung zad 'dir bkod la / /
nongs par mchis rnams mkhas pa'i spyan sngar bshags / /
dge 'dis mtshon pa'i dus gsum dang 'brel ba'i / /
bdag gzhan dge ba'i rtsa ba bci mchis pa / /
gnas skabs zab mo'i don 'di legs rtogs nas / /
mar thug byang chub chen po myur 'thob shog /
de ma thob kyi tshe rabs thams cad du / /
blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan phyogs kun tu / /
bsgreng la sa steng 'gran zlam mchis pa'i / /
phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba 'thob par shog /
'di nyid 'chad dang nyan par byed pa rnams /
rgyal ba'i spyan sngar skyang bar zhal bzhes pa / /
zhing skyong gzi ldan dbang phyug 'khor bcas kyis / /
g.yal ba med par rtag tu grogs byed shog /
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan rtsa 'gral gyi spyi don rnam bshad snying po rgyan gyi snang ba zhes bya ba /
mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i dge slong dge 'dun bstan pa dar rgyal kyis mdzad pa'i skabs dang po'i rnam bshad bshad zin to / /

oM swasti /
'og min gnas su nges pa lnga ldan du / /
mngon par sang rgyas lnga bdo'i 'gro 'dren phyir /
|sgyu 'phrul las bltams rnam 'dren nyi ma'i gnyen / /
gang gi gsung rab sher phyin dgongs pa'i gnas / /
sbas don ji bzhin gsal mdzad mi pham mgon / /
thog med sku mched la sogs mkhas rnams kyi / /
zab rgyas legs bshad rin chen 'byung khung las / /
rnam bshad bsam 'phel dbang gi rgyal po rnyed / /
lung rigs dpyad gsum dag pa'i rnam dpyod kyis / /
thub bstan rgyal mtshan rtsar bkod rnam dkar mthus / /
rgyal bstan spyi dang rje btsun btsong kha pa'i / /
bshad sgrub bstan pa nam yang mi nub shog /
de nyid 'dzin pa'i rtsa lag rnam 'dren rje / /
phyag na padma'i sku tshe rab brten cing / /
bslabs gsum gter mdzod thos bsam nor bu'i gling / /
bshad sgrub sde bzhi'i 'phrin las rgyas par shog /
'di'i ched sgo gsum ngal ba bstan pa dang / /
bdag pa spel sogs mthun rkyan bsgrubs pa kun / /
gnas skabs lha mi'i srid pa rim brgyud de / /
ring min sku gsum thob pa'i rgyu ru bsngo / /
dge legs kun gyi 'byung gnas bla ma dang / /
dngos grub 'dzad med gtar gyur lhag pa'i lha / /
mthun @# / /
rkyen spel mdzad li byin lha ra ches / /
bsam don lhun grub bkra shis bde legs mdzod / /
ces bstan bcos sa chen po mngor par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi spyi don mkhas grub bstan pa dar rgyas kyis mdzad pa'i rnam bshad snyang po rgyan gyi snang ba zhes bya ba 'di snga sor ser smad rang du par zhin yod par snang yang lcags sbrul la zhugs kyis rkyen dbang du song ba bcas /
spyi don gyi bstan bcos 'di bzhin blo gsal rnams la phan thogs che nges yod stabs bstan rgyun la bsams gzhung sa nas par gsar bskrun bgyid rtsis yod thog rgyal khab pi cing nas g.yung dgon khri pa rgyud stong shar pa chas rjes kyang bskul ma'i nyer len la brten sngon yod par ma la yig nor phran bu yod 'dug ba rnams rang lugs khas len dang mthun khyad ser smad thos bsam nor bu'i gling gi slob dpon las thog pa grags pa 'phrin las nas zhag 'jug bgyis shing /
dge bshes rab 'byams pa rin chen rgyal mtshan dang /
dka' bcu 'phrin las chos 'khor gnyis nas kyang ched du yig char dag ther skyo sel legs par byas /
do dam rtse drung spyang grong bskal bzang 'phrin las yar 'phel dang /
e snye'i bris brkos mkhas bsdus bzhi bcu skor nas me khyi lo 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gi gzhal mang khang phe brang chen po po ta lar par gsar bsgrun bgyis dus bar byang smon tshig tu shAkya'i dge slong da mo no mon han ngag dbang 'jam dpal bde legs rgya mtshos dga' ldan bg+sang sngags dga' tshal gyi gtsug lag khang du sbyar ba 'dis kyang rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che phyogs dus gnas skabs thams cad du dang zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas pa'i rgyur gyur cig /
